- Perform operator activities with a primary and secondary operator model: In this model, the secondary operator opens the door and hands material to the primary operator who only operates within the Grade A space. (See Topic 9.)

            
- The RABS design should consider, under a risk assessment, a zone of protection using an UDAF unit to at least cover the open-door radius. The positions have to be determined by a risk analysis and should consider frequent open-door activities such as the setup of stopper bowls or feeding lanes. Figure 1.8-1 shows an example for UDAF extension (1, 9).

            
- Evaluate the need to take additional (continuous) air samples (viable and total particulates) in the Grade B area with UDAF immediately surrounding the open-door area for the duration of the open-door setup activities (1, 9). (See PDA Technical Report No. 62: Recommended Practices for Manual Aseptic Processes for additional guidance for personnel behavior.)

            
- AVS qualification should be done to ensure that there is a UDAF flush away and out of the RABS during setup.

            
- Evaluate the possibility of performing VPHP decontamination after setup (cRABS or oRABS with cleanroom).

            
- After setup, the use of automatic decontamination reduces the risk of ingress of the operator into Grade A.

        

        

**Rationale**

        

Open-door activities typically necessary for equipment setup are of a higher risk as personnel must ingress into the Grade A space. All activities that minimize the risk of introducing bioburden into the Grade A environment will reduce the risk to the environment and, subsequently, the product. Such activities include, but are not limited to, the following:

        

            
- Minimizing the number of open doors to reduce the potential disruption of the UDAF within the RABS.

            
- Maintaining protective covers on equipment, such as bonnets on a stopper bowl, keeps the sterilized surfaces from being exposed until the RABS doors have been closed and ensuring greater protection. It also allows for the door-open time to be minimized, completing the setup activities through the glove ports in a second step (4).

            
- The utilization of additional protective measures (sterile sleeves, longer gloves, etc.) needs to be evaluated based upon an approved risk assessment.

            
- Similarly, the primary/secondary operator model safeguards the integrity of the gowning of the primary operator, further reducing the risk of introducing contamination. (See PDA TR-62 for additional information.)

            
- Having UDAF immediately adjacent to the doors, so that once the door is open, the area remains covered by Grade B surrounding the open door, will reduce the risk of introducing bioburden into the RABS enclosure.

        

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**設置（Setup）階段**是 RABS 運營中風險最高的時段之一，因為操作員必須進入 Grade A 區域安裝設備元件（如充填針頭、塞子碗、導軌等）。與充填期間的介入不同，設置通常**無法完全避免開門操作**。

            

**"Top Down" Approach（由上而下組裝法）：**先安裝上方元件，再安裝下方元件，確保安裝動作不會發生在已暴露的關鍵表面上方。這是一個簡單但極為有效的污染風險控制策略。

            

**Primary/Secondary Operator Model（主/副操作員模式）：**副操作員負責開門和傳遞物料，主操作員專注於 Grade A 區域內的操作。這樣可以保護主操作員的更衣完整性，因為他/她不需要觸碰門把或 Grade B 區域的物品。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

設置階段就像**搬家到一間已消毒的手術室**：你必須把家具（設備元件）搬進去，但每次開門都會讓走廊的灰塵進來。最聰明的做法是：

            

                
- 家具先用塑膠膜包好（保護罩/無菌盒），進門後再拆

                
- 一次只開一扇門（避免對流）

                
- 先放天花板的燈具，再放桌子（由上而下）

                
- 門口有一個人接應（副操作員），裡面的人專心擺放（主操作員）

                
- 搬完後用消毒噴霧清一遍（VPHP 生物去污）

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Legacy Systems（舊式系統）的挑戰：**文件特別提到，對於舊系統可能無法在關門後透過手套口移除保護罩的情況，需要制定替代方案並記錄在 CCS 中。這表示法規單位認可不同設備能力的差異，但**不接受「做不到所以不做」**的態度 -- 必須有書面的替代方案和風險評估。

            

**VPHP 設置後去污：**cRABS 的一個重要優勢是可以在設置完成後執行 VPHP 自動生物去污。這一步驟能大幅降低設置階段引入的微生物風險，相當於給 Grade A 區域做了一次「重置」。oRABS 如果配合潔淨室也可以考慮這一做法。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**設置階段風險降低檢查清單：**

            

                
- 所有可滅菌的元件是否已在滅菌前預組裝？

                
- 所有滅菌品是否有保護罩/無菌盒？保護罩是否設計為可在閉門後透過手套口移除？

                
- 組裝順序是否遵循「由上而下」原則？

                
- UDAF 覆蓋範圍是否涵蓋所有需要開門的區域？

                
- 是否有設置後 VPHP 去污的能力（cRABS）？

                
- 操作員是否穿戴額外的無菌保護裝備（無菌袖套、加長手套）？

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼「一次只開一扇門」對維持 UDAF 氣流模式至關重要？如果同時開兩扇門會發生什麼？

                
2. 主/副操作員模式如何比單人操作提供更高的無菌保證？從更衣完整性的角度分析。

                
3. 比較 cRABS 和 oRABS 在設置後生物去污能力方面的差異，以及這對 CCS 策略的影響。

            

        

    

Q 1.9 What construction design considerations are required for materials and maintenance?

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Recommendation**

        

RABS surfaces should be manufactured in materials compatible with the environmental classification conditions required for the proposed use.

        

**Construction Materials Considerations:**

        

            
- Interior metallic surfaces in direct or indirect contact with the primary packing should be constructed in 316 stainless steel or better and, for the rest of the line, metallic components could be constructed of low-carbon 304 stainless steel or better (1, 6).

            
- Interior transparent surfaces made of polycarbonate or glass.

            
- Seals joining the RABS with upstream and downstream equipment should take temperature and differential pressures into consideration (e.g., depyrogenation tunnel to filler RABS or freeze dryer).

            
- Cleanable with detergents commonly used in the cleanroom with no absorbing or desorbing effect when in contact with them (10).

        

        

All RABS surfaces should be resistant to the following conditions and agents to avoid the release of particles:

        

            
- Scratches and abrasions.

            
- Detergents and sporicidals used for CIP and cleaning-out-of-place, or disinfection (e.g., turntables, guides) (11).

            
- Sterilization process as SIP for fixed-system components (e.g., filling path).

            
- External sterilization processes with moist heat or radiation, or chemical sterilization processes for complementary components removable from RABS (e.g., stopper bowl, feeding lanes), or ready to use.

        

        

**Maintenance Considerations**

        

The internal RABS working areas should be designed to minimize the risk of contamination in critical zones for troubleshooting and repair activities.

        

The access to maintenance panels and/or mechanical spaces should be outside the RABS and below the operating/processing level (product height) as much as possible. Even if outside of the machine, these areas should not be opened without additional controls being evaluated and implemented (e.g., requires to exchange gowning after those activities).

        

All maintenance activities for a RABS and related equipment should be scheduled in a plan to occur at the same time, when it is possible, to avoid multiple preventive-maintenance work-order days.

        

**Rationale**

        

The RABS and equipment construction materials should be designed to meet such production requirements as cleanability, sanitization, and practicality of use, with the scope to reduce the contamination risk by particles that could be released from routine use or from eventual damages and abrasion occurred during routine production or maintenance activities.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**316 vs. 304 不鏽鋼的選擇邏輯：**

            

                
- **316SS（含鉬）：**用於與產品直接或間接接觸的表面。鉬元素提供更強的抗氯化物腐蝕能力，適合頻繁使用消毒劑和 SIP 蒸汽滅菌的環境。

                
- **304SS（低碳）：**用於產線其餘非直接接觸產品的金屬元件。成本較低但仍具備基本的耐腐蝕性。

            

            

**Hygienic Design（衛生設計）：**所有表面必須可清潔、不會吸收或釋放化學物質、能承受反覆的消毒和滅菌處理而不產生微粒。這是 GMP 對製藥設備的基本要求。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

選擇 RABS 建材就像**選擇餐廳廚房的檯面材質**：你不會用木頭（會吸水、藏菌），而是用不鏽鋼。但如果這個廚房每天用強酸清潔劑洗，你就需要更高等級的不鏽鋼（316SS）來防止腐蝕。至於客人看得到的透明隔板，就像壽司店的玻璃展示櫃一樣，用聚碳酸酯或玻璃。

            

維護面板放在 RABS 外面且低於產品高度，就像餐廳把水管維修口設在廚房外面的牆壁底部 -- 修水管時不會影響到料理檯面上的食材。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**密封件的溫度/壓差考量：**RABS 與上下游設備（如除熱原隧道、凍乾機）的連接密封件必須同時承受高溫（SIP）和壓差條件。這是設計中容易被忽略但在運行中經常出問題的地方。密封件失效會導致 Grade A 環境的完整性喪失。

            

**維護活動集中排程：**PDA 建議將所有維護活動安排在同一時間執行，避免多次維護導致多次潛在的污染暴露。這是一個務實的建議 -- 每次維護都需要額外的清潔和可能的重新確效，集中執行能大幅減少停機時間。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼維護面板的位置要設在 RABS 外部且低於產品操作高度？如果維護面板在 RABS 內部，會對 CCS 產生什麼影響？

                
2. 列出 RABS 表面需要承受的化學品和物理條件清單。哪些材質要求對於 cRABS 比 oRABS 更為嚴格？為什麼？

                
3. 當你評估一個 RABS 供應商的設計方案時，你會從哪些方面檢查其「衛生設計」的合規性？

            

        

    

Q 1.10 What unique design provisions are required for highly potent compounds exposed within closed restricted access barrier systems (cRABS)?

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Recommendation**

        

**Environmental Health Safety vs. Good Manufacturing Practices**

        

When designing a RABS for aseptic highly potent compounds, both the good manufacturing practice (GMP) and environmental health and safety (EHS) aspects are very important. While overpressure of the containment is necessary from a GMP perspective, negative pressure is required from the EHS standpoint to ensure operator safety (6).

        

Therefore, the pressure differential between the inside of the RABS and the outside environment must be positive. To avoid contamination from the most highly potent exposure area (e.g., filling zone), this zone is operated in negative pressure towards adjacent RABS sections. To make this physically and technically possible, a cRABS is needed. To allow for the creation and maintenance of the pressure differences during operation, it needs at least a cRABS, if recirculating air is used, a dedicated air handling unit (AHU) must be present.

        

**Additional Considerations:**

        

            
- Ability to safely change out terminal HEPAs by a safe-change filter system or one-pass aeration systems (with bag-in/bag-out exhaust HEPAs) (See Figure 1.10-1.)

            
- Interlocked door sensors and other mechanical devices to ensure operator safety

            
- Vacuum systems should be avoided where possible; otherwise, the integration of filters that prevent contamination at the base of the machine should be considered

            
- Transfer ports should be present to manage the removal of contained material used for spillage clean-up without having to open the RABS.*

            
- Pressure differential-monitoring systems to alarm in case of loss of pressure differential or RABS leakage.

            
- Double glass doors are to be avoided (See Figure 1.10-1.)

            
- Important for the commissioning of such products is the correct protective equipment of the employees and their behavior in case of an accidental breach.

        

        

**Note: This consideration does not apply for monitoring equipment using vacuum, such as total-particle counters or active viable monitoring. The monitoring equipment must be located in the most critical positions according to the EM risk analysis. A strategy to prevent contamination of the vacuum lines and the monitoring equipment must be evaluated (e.g., the particulate filter above the machine plate in the aseptic area) immediately after the sampling head for active viable (6). The sampling head must be treated as any other exposed equipment surface within the RABS and needs to be appropriately cleaned before the sterilization cycle. For particulate measurement systems, a different strategy must be considered. Total particle counters should be dedicated to certain areas and changed in situ to reduce the movement of the equipment and to limit exposure. Particulate filter can be placed after the device to ensure contamination prevention of the vacuum lines and pumps.*

        

**Cleaning**

        

A highly preferred method for cleaning a cRABS contaminated with toxic substances is the automatic wash-in-place (WIP) process. The WIP process can either be executed with spray guns mounted inside the RABS for manual wash-down or with a spray ball to achieve an automatic wash down. This means that even hard-to-reach areas can be cleaned more easily while the doors remain closed and, therefore, the risk of operator exposure is minimized. The handling of the wastewater must be considered with a special focus on the draining systems (i.e., EU Annex 1: Manufacture of Sterile Medicinal Products excludes drains in Grade A or Grade B environments) and toxic water separation. Depending on toxicity, measuring residuals in wastewater is recommended to ensure the RABS environment is free from potential potent residuals. A risk assessment should be performed to determine the proper neutralization of the wastewater from the toxic process and proper design. Nevertheless, the machine and the containment must, of course, be designed in such a way that all parts can be easily cleaned and equipped in a hygienic design.

        

**Rationale**

        

Potent compounds are hazardous to operators and, while product sterility must be maintained, it is equally important to ensure that operators and the environment they operate in can be protected from exposure. Utilization of cRABS, with negative pressure and WIP systems, allows for the operation and cleaning of the system, without ever exposing the operator or the environment outside of the RABS to the compound.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**GMP vs. EHS 的壓力矛盾：**這是處理高效價化合物（如 ADC 藥物偶聯物、細胞毒性藥物）時最經典的設計難題。

            

                
- **GMP 要求：**RABS 相對於外部環境必須**正壓**，防止外部微生物進入 Grade A

                
- **EHS 要求：**含毒性物質的區域必須**負壓**，防止有毒物質外洩傷害操作員

            

            

**解決方案（壓力梯度設計）：**

            

                
- RABS 整體相對於背景環境保持正壓（滿足 GMP）

                
- 充填區（最高暴露區域）相對於 RABS 其他區段保持負壓（滿足 EHS）

                
- 這種「局部負壓+整體正壓」的設計只有 cRABS 能實現，因為需要密封性和獨立空調系統

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像一座處理**放射性物質的醫院**：整棟醫院相對於外部保持正壓（防止外部髒空氣進入），但放射科的操作室相對於走廊保持負壓（防止放射性物質外洩到走廊）。這就是「整體正壓、局部負壓」的概念。

            

WIP 系統就像把一台**自動洗車機**裝在 RABS 裡面 -- 車門不用打開，內部的噴頭就能把所有有毒殘留物沖洗乾淨。廢水還要經過專門的處理系統，不能直接排入一般下水道。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**為什麼只有 cRABS 適用？**oRABS 無法維持密封性和壓力梯度，因此無法同時滿足 GMP 正壓和 EHS 局部負壓的要求。對於高效價化合物充填，cRABS 是最低要求（隔離器則是更優選擇）。

            

**EU Annex 1 排水限制：**歐盟法規禁止在 Grade A 和 Grade B 環境中設置排水口。因此，WIP 系統的廢水管理是一個重大設計挑戰 -- 需要特殊的廢水收集和中和系統，且不能使用傳統地漏。

            

**Safe-Change HEPA Filter System：**更換被有毒物質污染的 HEPA 濾網時，必須使用 Bag-In/Bag-Out（BIBO）系統，確保操作員不會暴露於污染的濾網。這是生物安全實驗室和核設施常用的技術。

        

        

            

#### 壓力梯度設計邏輯

            

```

壓力梯度示意：

外部環境（Grade B）: 基準壓力 P0
        |
        v  (+15 Pa)
RABS 外圍區段:      P0 + 15 Pa
        |
        v  (-10 Pa)
充填區（高暴露區）:   P0 + 5 Pa

結果：
- 充填區 > 外部環境 (+5 Pa) --> GMP 正壓要求 OK
- 充填區 < RABS 外圍 (-10 Pa) --> EHS 負壓防護 OK
            
```

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果你的 CDMO 需要在現有 oRABS 產線上充填一種 OEL < 1 μg/m³ 的高效價 ADC 藥物，你會建議什麼樣的設備升級方案？

                
2. 為什麼文件建議避免使用真空系統？在必須使用時（如粒子計數器），應採取什麼防護措施？

                
3. 解釋為什麼「雙層玻璃門」在高效價化合物 cRABS 中應被避免。從清潔性和密封性的角度思考。

            

        

    

Q 1.11 What are the best engineering design considerations for in-line environmental monitoring (EM)?

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Recommendation**

        

Monitoring should be performed at locations posing the highest risk of contamination of the sterile equipment surfaces, containers, closures, and product. The selection of monitoring locations and the orientation and positioning of sampling devices should be justified in an EM risk analysis and appropriate to obtain reliable data from the critical zones (1, 4, 12).

        

**In-line Viable Monitoring:**

        

            
- Viable air samplers located near critical process zones (e.g., accumulation table, filling station, stoppering section).

            
- Consider location near glove ports for ease of plate placement, removal, and storage.

            
- Consider installing an EM plate holder for staging multiple EM plates as well as holding the lid of the air sampler, if applicable. This stand should be installed near to the air sampler and within reach via glove ports.

            
- Verify active air samplers are part of the calibration program (airflow).

            
- Consider First Air requirements for critical surfaces (e.g., initial load of agar plates, replacement of settle plates).

        

        

**In-line Total Particulate Monitoring:**

        

            
- Total particle air sampler located near critical process zones within a one foot radius of the working position (e.g., accumulation table, filling, stoppering) (4).

            
- If air samplers have covers, verify sampler is near glove ports for ease of cover placement or removal.

            
- Verify air sampler is part of the calibration program (airflow, particulates typically 0.5 μm and 5.0 μm).

            
- Ensure that the tube between the sampling probe (isokinetic funnel) and particle counter is <1 m minimizing bends or radii. If deviating from this requirement, particle loss studies need to demonstrate the functionality (1).

        

        

**If considering the use of an alternate rapid microbiological methods (real-time monitoring via biofluorescent particle-counting), considerations should include, but not be limited to, the following (1, 6, 12, 13):**

        

            
- Sampling locations must be representative and close to conventional settle plates to show equivalency of the system for validation and data collection during production.

            
- Suitable installation location of the counter to ensure accessibility for retraction of gelatine filter/agar plate for possibility of identifying the autofluorescence unit.

            
- Tube length from sampling point to counter needs to be considered and validated by particle loss studies if >1 m.

            
- Alarm management for autofluorescence unit hit must be in place and validated.

        

        

**Temp/RH/DP/Airflow Velocity (6):**

        

            
- Sensors should be placed in representative locations—located downstream of UDAF/HEPA filters but above product pathway—so as not to interfere with equipment operation and potential interventions.

        

        

**Alarm and Notification Systems:**

        

            
- Warnings (alerts and alarms) should be in place to alert operators in the event of any deviations from the predefined EM parameters.

            
- Where alarm delays are utilized, a duration of delay must be justified.

        

        

**Data Analysis and Reporting:**

        

            
- Consider having the inline EM sensors integral to the RABS control system to facilitate central operator control and integration of EM readings to equipment interlocks (e.g., high particle counts halts filling).

            
- Alert levels should be established, and then trended, followed by periodic review.

        

        

**Rationale**

        

EM should effectively evaluate the state of environmental conditions within the RABS (e.g., total particulates, viables, air quality, airflow and pressure cascade).

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Environmental Monitoring（環境監測）**是 RABS 設計中容易被低估的領域。EM 不只是「放幾個培養皿」，而是一個完整的**工程設計問題**，涉及採樣位置、管路長度、校準程序、警報系統和數據整合。

            

**關鍵設計原則：**

            

                
- **位置選擇：**監測點必須位於污染風險最高的位置（充填站、加塞區、積瓶台），而非最方便安裝的位置

                
- **可及性：**EM 設備必須可透過手套口操作（更換培養皿、蓋板等），否則每次操作都需要開門

                
- **管路限制：**粒子計數器的採樣管長度 <1 m 且應避免彎折，否則會造成粒子損失導致數據不可靠

                
- **等速吸引（Isokinetic Sampling）：**採樣探頭的進氣速度必須與周圍氣流速度匹配

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

EM 系統就像一間房子的**煙霧偵測器和空氣品質監測器**。你不會把煙霧偵測器放在沒有電器的儲藏室（低風險區），而是放在廚房和臥室（高風險區）。而且偵測器不能裝在通風口正前方（會被吹散煙霧導致漏報），也不能距離太遠（反應太慢）。

            

粒子計數器的採樣管 <1 m 限制，就像你用一根很長的吸管喝珍珠奶茶 -- 管子越長、轉彎越多，珍珠（粒子）就越容易卡在中間，你喝到的（偵測到的）就越少。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**即時微生物監測的未來趨勢：**文件提到了生物螢光粒子計數（Biofluorescent Particle Counting）作為替代性快速微生物方法（RMM）。這項技術可以實現**即時連續**的活性微生物監測，不再依賴培養皿更換（培養皿更換本身就是一次介入）。

            

但法規上仍要求新方法必須與傳統沉降板方法進行等效性驗證，採樣位置必須接近常規沉降板以進行比對。

            

**EM 與設備聯鎖：**將 EM 數據整合到 RABS 控制系統中（例如，高粒子數自動停止充填）是一個先進且有價值的設計理念。這實現了從「被動監測」到「主動控制」的轉變，大幅提升無菌保證水平。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**EM 設計審查場景：**你正在審查供應商提交的 RABS EM 設計方案。以下是你應檢查的關鍵項目：

            
                
| 檢查項目 | 合格標準 |
| --- | --- |
                
| 活性空氣採樣器位置 | 位於關鍵製程區域附近，可透過手套口操作 |
                
| 粒子計數器採樣管長度 | <1 m，最少彎折；若超過需有粒子損失研究 |
                
| EM 培養皿架 | 安裝於採樣器附近，手套口可及範圍內 |
                
| 溫度/濕度/壓差感測器 | 位於 HEPA 下游但在產品路徑上方 |
                
| 警報系統 | 已定義警報延遲時間並有書面理由 |
                
| 數據整合 | EM 數據可與設備控制系統聯鎖 |
            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼粒子計數器的採樣管長度被限制在 1 公尺以內？如果你的設備佈局使得管長必須超過 1 m，你需要做什麼額外的驗證工作？

                
2. 「高粒子數自動停止充填」的聯鎖設計可能帶來什麼好處和潛在問題？考慮假陽性警報的影響。

                
3. 比較傳統沉降板監測和生物螢光即時監測在 RABS 環境中的優缺點，特別是對介入頻率的影響。

            

        

    

Q 1.12 What are the criteria for retrofitting and design considerations for restricted access barrier systems (RABS), including RABS interfaces?

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Recommendation**

        

Retrofitting a line into a RABS is normally a temporary solution to maintain compliance with GMP. However, retrofitting can be beneficial by increasing sterility assurance while the company works on the longer-term implementation of a full RABS or isolator design.

        

Typical retrofit scenarios, include:

        

            
- Conventional A/B filling to oRABS

            
- oRABS to cRABS

        

        

Note: Retrofitting a cRABS could be challenging.

        

            
- Adding transfer interfaces (e.g. RTPs) to existing RABS

        

        

Retrofitting a RABS or transferring system interfaces along the filling line is recommended to address the following needs:

        

            
- Create a barrier system for the RABS critical zone and interfaces

            
- Compliance with First Air concepts (i.e., modifications to the design of the manufacturing line may be needed)

            
- Reduced open-door interventions

            
- Improved CCS for the manufacturing line

            
- Requirements from relevant health authorities (international and local)

        

        

Note: Retrofitting a RABS could be difficult.

        

**Points to consider for a retrofitting approach include, but are not limited to, the following:**

        

**First Air Principle Maintained**

        

Check the feasibility of any operation that must be performed with doors closed to ensure that unidirectionality (First Air Principle) can be maintained during the manipulation. Also consider the use of components and materials that can be transferred into the RABS via rapid transfer ports (e.g. RTPs) to avoid the necessity to open the barrier doors. These ports should be located nearest to the use of the materials transferred in. Port location and First Air verification can be accomplished via the use of a 3-D model with computational fluid dynamics (CFD) or a mock-up model prior to the retrofit. Refer to Questions 1.2 and 1.3 for further details on RABS design considerations.

        

**Production Operations**

        

Ensure full filling equipment access via glove ports for aseptic connection and interventions in critical zones, reducing the door opening for intervention during production. It is important to ensure that interventions during all phases of production are evaluated including batch setup. Refer to Question 9.2 for further details on the qualification of interventions.

        

For the differential pressure requirement associated with, for example, a Load Accumulation Table to Transfer Cart RABS interface (Grade B background), the background environment is the Grade B area with the Grade A Load Unload Automatic Transfer representing the critical zone. Consequently, at the interface, a positive airflow from the critical zones (i.e., RABS) to the supporting background environment (i.e., Grade B area) is required.

        

Minimize or consider the possibility of eliminating operator intervention during the freeze-dryer loading/unloading, implementing automatic or semi-automatic loading system, that can provide:

        

            
- Creation of a barrier system

            
- First Air concept compliance

        

        

Retrofitting a RABS for a freeze-dryer loading/unloading system could be realized in a first step by a semi-automatic system before changing to a fully automated system.

        

**Rationale**

        

When retrofitting, the design of the RABS must work around the existing design of the filling equipment. It is important, and challenging, to achieve a balance between ensuring the retrofit allows sufficient access to perform all required interventions while also minimizing the need to perform open-door activities/interventions.

        

In a RABS retrofit, the design of the unidirectional airflow protection surrounding the RABS barrier can also be a challenge, and it is important to ensure that it can cover the entire area exposed during the opening of doors (i.e., Grade B).

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Retrofitting（改裝）：**將現有的充填線升級為 RABS 的過程。這不是最理想的方案（全新設計更佳），但對於需要在短期內提升 GMP 合規性的工廠來說，是一個務實的過渡策略。

            

**典型升級路徑：**

            

                
- **傳統 A/B 充填 → oRABS：**最常見的改裝場景。在現有充填線周圍加裝屏障面板和門。

                
- **oRABS → cRABS：**難度更高，需要增加密封性、可能需要獨立空調系統。

                
- **加裝 RTP：**在現有 RABS 上增加快速傳遞口，減少開門需求。

            

            

**介面設計（Interface Design）：**RABS 與上下游設備（如除熱原隧道、凍乾機、傳輸車）的連接點是改裝設計中最關鍵的部分，必須確保壓力梯度和 First Air 原則在介面處不被破壞。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

RABS 改裝就像**在一棟已建成的房子上加裝氣密窗和空調系統**。你不能拆掉整棟房子重建（成本太高、停產太久），但你可以逐步升級：先把普通窗戶換成氣密窗（加裝屏障面板），然後加裝全熱交換器（壓差控制），再裝一個傳遞窗口（RTP），這樣送外賣的人不用每次都開大門。

            

最大的挑戰是：房子的格局已經固定了，你必須在現有空間內想辦法。有時候窗戶的位置不適合裝氣密窗（手套口位置受限），有時候牆壁太薄裝不了傳遞窗口（結構限制）。這就是為什麼文件提到「改裝可能很困難」。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**CFD 模擬在改裝中的價值：**在改裝前使用 3-D 模型和計算流體力學（CFD）模擬是極為重要的步驟。因為改裝後的 RABS 幾何形狀往往不如全新設計那麼理想（可能有突出物、不規則的轉角），氣流模式可能會出現意料之外的紊流或死角。CFD 模擬可以在實際改裝前識別這些問題。

            

**凍乾機裝/卸料的改裝策略：**文件建議採用分階段方法 -- 先實施半自動系統，再過渡到全自動系統。這是一個務實的建議，因為凍乾機裝卸料是 RABS 充填線中最複雜的介面之一，涉及大量容器的移動和溫度管控。

            

**法規驅動的改裝：**許多改裝計劃是由衛生主管機關的要求（如 FDA 483 觀察項或 EU Annex 1 更新後的合規差距）驅動的。改裝方案必須記錄在 CCS 中，並作為長期屏障技術升級計劃的一部分。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**場景：**你的 CDMO 收到 FDA 的 483 觀察項，指出你的傳統 A/B 充填線需要升級到屏障技術。管理層決定先改裝為 oRABS 作為過渡方案，同時規劃 3 年後的隔離器新線。你的改裝設計檢查清單：

            

                
- 現有充填設備的尺寸和佈局是否允許加裝屏障面板？

                
- 手套口位置是否能覆蓋所有必要的介入操作？（用 Mock-up 驗證）

                
- UDAF 覆蓋範圍是否足以涵蓋開門區域？

                
- 是否能加裝 RTP 以減少開門頻率？

                
- 與凍乾機/隧道的介面壓力梯度是否可以實現？

                
- CFD 模擬是否已驗證改裝後的氣流模式？

                
- 改裝方案是否已記錄在 CCS 中，並有明確的長期升級時間表？

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼文件兩次強調「改裝可能很困難」？從 First Air 原則、手套口定位和壓差控制三個角度分析改裝的主要技術挑戰。

                
2. 比較「傳統 A/B → oRABS」和「oRABS → cRABS」兩種改裝場景在技術難度和成本上的差異。

                
3. 凍乾機裝卸料區的 RABS 改裝為什麼特別具有挑戰性？從容器移動、溫度控制和介面壓差的角度分析。

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **Q1.7 開門介入預防：**RABS 的核心設計目標是作為封閉系統運行。當閉門介入可行時，開門介入**必須被禁止**。透過 RTP、自動化、機器人系統和合理的手套口佈置，可以在設計階段消除大部分開門需求。不可避免的開門介入需要嚴格的程序控制，包括 AVS 預評估、偏差評估、消毒、批次隔離考量，以及 Grade A 條件恢復確認。

        
- **Q1.8 設置風險最小化：**設置階段是 RABS 運營中風險最高的時期。關鍵緩解措施包括：一次只開一扇門、使用保護罩/無菌盒、由上而下組裝法、主/副操作員模式、UDAF 延伸覆蓋開門區域，以及設置後的 VPHP 自動生物去污。

        
- **Q1.9 建材與維護：**產品接觸面使用 316SS、非接觸面使用 304SS、透明面使用聚碳酸酯或玻璃。所有材質必須耐化學消毒和滅菌。維護面板應設在 RABS 外部且低於產品高度，維護活動應集中排程。

        
- **Q1.10 高效價化合物：**處理高效價化合物時需要同時滿足 GMP（正壓）和 EHS（局部負壓）要求，只有 cRABS 能實現這種壓力梯度設計。WIP 系統允許在閉門狀態下清洗有毒殘留，廢水管理需特別注意 EU Annex 1 的排水限制。

        
- **Q1.11 線上環境監測：**EM 設備必須安裝在污染風險最高的位置。粒子計數器採樣管 <1 m、活性空氣採樣器可透過手套口操作、即時生物螢光監測是未來趨勢。EM 數據應整合到 RABS 控制系統實現設備聯鎖（如高粒子數自動停機）。

        
- **Q1.12 改裝設計：**改裝是提升合規性的過渡方案，典型路徑為傳統 A/B → oRABS 或 oRABS → cRABS。改裝前應使用 CFD 模擬驗證氣流，確保 First Air 原則、手套口可及性和壓差梯度在改裝後仍能維持。凍乾機介面是改裝中最複雜的區域，建議分階段從半自動過渡到全自動。

    

    

PDA Points to Consider No. 12 (2025): Restricted Access Barrier Systems

    

Section 1b: Topic 1 RABS Design (Q1.7 - Q1.12) | p23 - p33

    

Educational Material for CDMO Professionals

## Topic 2: Physical Environment 物理環境 (p34-p40)

# Topic 2: Physical Environment

    

主題二：物理環境

    

PDA Points to Consider No. 12 (2025) - RABS | p34 - p40

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 瞭解 RABS 周圍房間的最低環境分級要求（Grade B），以及為何不能低於此等級

        
- 理解 RABS 延伸單向氣流 (Extended UDAF) 區域的環境監測標準與策略

        
- 掌握氣流型態可視化研究 (AVS) 的完整執行方法論，包括煙霧產生、攝影記錄與實務考量

        
- 認識設施佈局設計中人員通過 Grade A RABS 區域的工程解決方案與風險緩解措施

    

    

### 本節目錄 Table of Contents

    

        Q 2.1 房間分級
        Q 2.2 延伸 UDAF 環境監測
        Q 2.3 氣流可視化研究 (AVS)
        Q 2.4 人員通道設計
    

## Q 2.1 Room Classification Surrounding RABS

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

### Q 2.1. What should be the classification of the room surrounding the restricted access barrier system (RABS)?

        

**Recommendation**

        

The minimum classification of the room immediately surrounding the RABS must be Grade B. However, a manufacturer may also choose to maintain these areas at more stringent levels of control when assessed for risk, especially in the area immediately surrounding the RABS doors, which may require execution of open-door interventions (i.e., during setup or filling) (1, 4).

        

**Rationale**

        

A RABS provides an enclosed and separated environment designed to reduce the risk of contamination to product, components, and product-contact surfaces when compared to conventional "curtained" aseptic processing operations. However, RABS are not fully sealed from the immediate surrounding environment and, in some designs, allow for open-door interventions by aseptic operators. As such, the adjacent background cleanroom environment must be appropriately classified and maintained to protect the critical processing zone(s) within the RABS; therefore, the cleanroom environment should not be lower than Grade B.

        

Companies should provide the maximum assurance possible and practicable so that the controlled RABS environment is not impacted by the surrounding environmental conditions since the RABS is not completely isolated from the surroundings, unlike closed isolators, for example.

        

            "Note: The minimum regulatory expectations (e.g., FDA, EMA) for the classification of manufacturing spaces immediately adjacent (i.e., background) to the Grade A critical processing zone is Grade B."
        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Grade B (B 級潔淨區)：**這是 RABS 周圍環境的最低分級要求。Grade B 區域在靜態（at rest）條件下需達到接近 Grade A 的微粒標準，在動態（in operation）條件下則有較寬鬆但仍嚴格的限值。

            

**RABS vs. Isolator (隔離器) 的關鍵差異：**RABS 並非完全密封的系統——它與周圍環境之間存在空氣交換路徑。這正是為何背景環境必須維持高等級的根本原因。隔離器則是完全密封的，因此其背景環境可降至 Grade C 甚至 Grade D。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像 RABS 就像一間有紗窗的手術室——紗窗（屏障）能擋住大部分污染物，但並非完全密封。因此，手術室外面的走廊（背景環境）也必須保持相當的清潔度。如果走廊髒亂不堪，即使有紗窗，灰塵和微生物仍會透過縫隙進入手術區域。而隔離器則像太空站——完全密封，外面是真空也無所謂。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**法規底線：**FDA 和 EMA 均明確要求 Grade A 關鍵製程區域的背景環境最低為 Grade B。這不是建議，而是強制性要求。

            

**風險加嚴原則：**文件特別提到，在 RABS 門附近可能需要執行開門操作的區域，廠商可能需要採用比 Grade B 更嚴格的管控。這體現了品質風險管理 (QRM) 的精神——根據實際風險調整管控等級。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 營運中，客戶常問：「我們的 RABS 產線背景環境是 Grade B 還是更高？」這會直接影響客戶對產品無菌保證的信心。如果 CDMO 能在門區域提供加嚴的環境控制（如額外的 UDAF 保護），將成為重要的競爭優勢，尤其是面對高價值生物製劑客戶時。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼 RABS 的背景環境不能像隔離器一樣降至 Grade C 或 Grade D？請從系統密封性的角度解釋。

                
2. 如果某間 CDMO 想在 RABS 門區域實施比 Grade B 更嚴格的控制，可以採取哪些具體措施？

            

        

    

## Q 2.2 Environmental Monitoring in Extended UDAF

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

### Q 2.2. Which environmental monitoring criteria are required in extended unidirectional airflow surrounding restricted access barrier system (RABS)?

        

**Recommendation**

        

Due to the presence of the UDAF around the open-door portion of the RABS, total particulates and viables should always reflect Grade A limits at the working position, at rest. Locations that are found to be critical based on the risk assessment, should have tighter limits than Grade B under the UDAF when the RABS door is in the open position, while in operation.

        

The remainder of the room should be subjected to sampling frequencies and limits (e.g., total particulates, viable air samples (active and passive)) and surface samples at a frequency appropriate for Grade B and adhering to Grade B limits.

        

**Rationale**

        

In the extended UDF surrounding the RABS, EM should be conducted to demonstrate the maintenance of a protective environment during the times when the doors are opened. The function of the extended UDF is to provide enhanced protection around critical zones where there is a break in the integrity of the Grade A RABS zone (i.e., during open-door interventions). During times when the doors are closed, this environment can be monitored as a more traditional Grade B environment, whereas during open-door interventions, it should be treated as an enhanced Grade B environment with limits (alert and action) defined based on a risk assessment.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Extended UDAF / UDF (延伸單向氣流)：**這是安裝在 RABS 門外側的額外單向氣流系統。當 RABS 門開啟時，此氣流形成一道「空氣帷幕」，防止背景環境的污染物進入 Grade A 區域。

            

**Enhanced Grade B (加嚴 B 級)：**這是一個介於 Grade A 和 Grade B 之間的監測概念。在開門操作期間，延伸 UDAF 區域不再適用普通的 Grade B 限值，而需要採用更嚴格的警戒與行動限值。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

延伸 UDAF 就像機場安檢區的「空氣門」(air curtain)——當商店大門打開時，空氣門會產生一道向下的氣流，阻止外面的熱空氣（或冷空氣）進入室內。同樣地，當 RABS 門開啟進行操作時，延伸 UDAF 就是那道阻擋外部污染的「空氣門」。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**雙重監測標準：**本文提出了一個重要的操作概念——同一個區域在不同操作狀態下需要不同的監測標準：

            

                
- **門關閉時：**按標準 Grade B 監測，使用 Grade B 限值

                
- **門開啟時：**按加嚴 Grade B 監測，使用基於風險評估定義的更嚴格的警戒與行動限值

            

            

這種動態監測策略反映了 EU Annex 1 (2022) 對 Contamination Control Strategy (CCS) 的要求——監測計畫必須與實際風險相匹配。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在實際 CDMO 營運中，建立「門開/門關」不同監測標準需要在 EM 程序文件中明確定義切換規則。建議在 SCADA/BMS 系統中整合門感測器，自動記錄門開啟時間，以便與 EM 數據進行關聯分析。這不僅是法規要求，也是數據完整性 (Data Integrity) 的體現。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼延伸 UDAF 區域在門開啟時不能直接套用 Grade A 限值？提示：考慮操作本身對環境的影響。

                
2. 如果在開門操作期間，延伸 UDAF 區域的微粒監測數據超出了「加嚴 Grade B」的行動限值，應該採取什麼措施？

            

        

    

## Q 2.3 Airflow Visualization Studies (AVS)

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

### Q 2.3. How should airflow pattern visualization/demonstration be performed in a restricted access barrier system (RABS) for airflow visualization studies (AVS)?

        

**Recommendation**

        

The purpose of airflow visualization studies (AVS) (also known as "smoke testing") is the verification of unidirectional airflow maintained during all required equipment functions and manual interventions. This is aligned to the principle of assuring First Air in contact with product and direct and indirect product-contact equipment. The intention is to demonstrate that all permitted interventions are appropriately designed and can be executed according to the approved methodology or procedure.

        

AVS should verify protective airflow is maintained at RABS entry 'mouseholes' without compromise to the process environment that protective airflow is applied to.

        

An additional reason to perform an AVS is to have a visual record of process operations conducted per requirements to allow the following:

        

            
- Used as training material to demonstrate correct process execution. An important aspect about AVS is that they should be exactly representatives of operational conditions, so people should have the right gowning, validated loads and packages should be used.

            
- Presenting to internal or external inspectors who may require visualization of a process that may not be (fully) running at the point of inspection.

            
- Assess EM sampling site locations and design of interventions or intervention discard strategies.

        

        

            "Note: It is important to know what the air velocity is at the working position during the airflow visualization testing so that a correlation can be established in routine requalification studies to demonstrate the continued applicability of the AVS."
        

        

**Airflow Pattern Visualization Process Activity Considerations**

        

It must be recognized that the act of performing airflow visualization disturbs the environment that it is designed to visualize due to the purposeful injection of a smoke or fogging spray into the critical zone that would self-evidently not occur during routine operations.

        

To minimize the impact of this disturbance in the air supplied to the RABS, the following should be considered:

        

            
1. **Develop a Qualification Protocol** — Work with affected departments (Manufacturing, Quality Assurance, Engineering, Microbiology) to determine and document the setup, operation, and intervention steps necessary for the process. The test objective is to show unidirectional airflow sweeping over critical surfaces.

            
2. **Select Smoke-Generation Equipment Type** (e.g., Fogger, Cartridge, Dry Ice) — There are multiple acceptable equipment options for the generation of "smoke" for airflow pattern visualization testing, including foggers that use dry ice, vaporization of water for injection (WFI) or deionized water, or liquid nitrogen. The use of foggers that generate glycerin-based vapor is not recommended because they can leave an oily residue on the test area, personnel, and/or floor areas.

            
3. **Select Water Vapor-Generating Equipment** — Water vapor-generating equipment has a variety of generation mechanisms and design styles, including cartridge-based (handheld) and continuous supply via external devices. Depending on the specifics of the application and the RABS design, one of these styles may be the better choice as there would be no residue formation.

            
4. **Amount of Smoke** — The amount of smoke generated should be sufficient to visualize the airflow (and possible turbulence), but not too much smoke to obscure the operators' actions or machine operations.

            
5. **Smoke Speed** — The smoke should be generated at slow speed in the opposite direction to the airflow, at approximately 45° against the direction of a vertical airflow and at a speed that minimizes disturbance. It should be noted that if the smoke flow was in the same direction as the normal airflow, that can reinforce the airflow directionality.

            
6. **Smoke Generator and Smoke Diffuser (i.e., Manifold)** — Movement of the smoke generator and smoke diffuser should be reduced to be as slow as possible, as recommended by good aseptic practices. To limit movements, the use of a smoke diffuser of sufficient size is suggested such that it becomes unnecessary to move it during the AVS.

            
7. **Smoke Generation Location** — The smoke is to be generated as high as possible above the working position, according to the design of the equipment, but not too close to the HEPA filter to avoid filter-clogging due to residue accumulation.

            
8. **Air Movement at Interfaces** — To check air movement at interfaces to the Grade B surrounding environment (e.g., when doors are open), the smoke is injected inside and outside the RABS. This is done at different locations to demonstrate the flush of the air from the Grade A RABS and its demonstrated unidirectionality (when injected inside) and the absence of air ingress (when injected from outside) into the RABS zone.

            
9. **Wall and Vertical Panel Considerations** — Injecting smoke near walls or vertical panels should be avoided, as this may create additional disturbances in airflow that would not occur in routine operations. Note: Air will flow slower along the RABS walls, and there will be minor eddies along the walls. This is to be expected by the application of physics.

            
10. **Airflow Visualization Study Frequency** — The frequency of re-executing an AVS is not timebound in the first instance; it should be based primarily on events (equipment or process change control). As periodic validation review is regarded as a qualification study, the study may need to be repeated for other reasons (e.g., improvements in film-capture quality over time).

            
11. **Open-door Intervention Considerations** — In the case of open-door interventions, airflow visualization qualification should be done to ensure that there is a unidirectional airflow flush away and out of the RABS during the intervention.

        

        

**Selection of Video Recording Equipment and Cinematography**

        

The record that exists after the execution of airflow visualization testing is a GMP record that assures the data integrity, a video record that may need to exist for many years. As such, careful thought must go into both the selection of the recording equipment and the modalities concerning film cinematography to maximize value of what is shown to the reviewer in the video footage. The following points and recommendations should be followed:

        

            
1. **Equipment and Physical Setup** — The equipment used and the physical setup to video-capture the performance of the airflow visualization testing must be considered to ensure that the record contains sufficient detail to demonstrate that unidirectional flow is maintained in all required areas. A good strategy to ensure this is to set up multiple cameras at different angles with significantly overlapping fields of view. Where applicable, built-in cameras and recording devices can be used to capture video of smoke studies; however, complete and detailed coverage of the study area must be accomplished.

            
2. **Visibility of Vapor on the Video Recording** — The rear glass doors of the RABS may need to be covered by an opaque backing or a contrasting color in order to facilitate visibility in the final video footage.

            
3. **Cinematography Considerations** — Contextualizing the cinematography by filming a timepiece that indicates the time and date before panning the camera to visualize the smoke directionality is recommended. Filming a schematic drawing of the RABS system and then the equipment section can also assist the viewer in this regard. Ensure that the differential pressure across the filter and velocity were within standard operating limits during the AVS. Each camera shot should be carefully prepared to ensure that no unnecessary activity is performed in the background. The video should be taken using two to four (2-4) different camera angles to facilitate, as much as possible, a three-dimensional view of the unidirectionality of airflow over the critical zones. Best practice is to synchronize the timing of all filmed scenes, so that direct comparison of the airflow visualization can be made from all filmed angles while viewing in a single pane. When footages are edited to be combined into one stream, the original video file, if considered to contain raw data, is to be retained.

        

        

**Practical Considerations**

        

Similarly, the logistics of the study execution require careful planning so that the captured film footage is integral and does not allow for any misinterpretation or gaps to the record. The following should be considered for implementation:

        

            
- Simulate a walk-through of interventions (dress rehearsal) to assist with seamless professional execution that minimizes the need for extensive editing. Consider the floor communication method (i.e., radios, hand signals) during execution if participating individuals are on opposite sides of a RABS.

            
- Simulate all manipulations strictly following good aseptic behavior, including glove decontamination, and limit the personnel in the space to the smoke-equipment operator, aseptic processing operators, video operator, and reviewer/approver.

            
- Filling line operation at maximum speed will require airflow visualization studies because of potential impact on protective airflows, including 'First air'.

            
- Consider bringing a cleanroom mobile device (e.g., tablet) to the film location so the video footage can be downloaded and reviewed by approvers on the floor immediately after the test study has been performed (subject to room classification).

            
- Verify that all support systems (e.g., room HVAC, unidirectional airflow) are in a controlled and qualified state and operational. Verify all personnel are present and gowned per routine procedure.

            
- Verify that the materials needed (i.e., smoke vapor source) are available and in sufficient quantities.

            
- Verify any smoke-detection equipment that could trigger an alarm and/or evacuation are switched off for the zone being filmed, in collaboration with the site security personnel. Particle and viable counters should be in operation to mimic the routine, but additional precautions may need to be taken to avoid damage to sensor heads.

            
- Verify that the room is in an acceptable state (i.e., normal housekeeping, no work in progress in the background of the video, no materials linked to shutdown activity stored in area being studied).

        

        

**Rationale**

        

Focus of the video reviewer may be diverted from the smoke study evaluation if simulated operations are not done with the expected level of control for the operation to be simulated (e.g., untidy areas, personnel not wearing required gowning). Additionally, abnormal conditions may not be considered representative of the routine when performing AVS.

        

The integrity of the airflow visualization film footage requires assurance (e.g., date, time, continuity, accuracy) for both inspectional and training purposes. The firm should assess periodically the need to repeat smoke testing to provide assurance that they reflect current operational characteristics.

        

This assessment should consider the following:

        

            
- Cumulative effect of process and/or facility changes

            
- Quality of the video footage being improved over time

            
- Improvements in the methodology of smoke generation and insertion techniques

        

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Airflow Visualization Studies / AVS (氣流可視化研究)：**俗稱「煙霧測試」(smoke testing)，透過在關鍵區域注入可見煙霧或霧氣，以視覺化方式驗證單向氣流 (UDAF) 是否在所有設備操作和人工介入期間維持正確方向。這是確認 First Air (初始空氣) 原則得到保障的核心驗證手段。

            

**First Air (初始空氣)：**直接從 HEPA 過濾器流出、未受任何阻擋或擾動的潔淨空氣。First Air 必須首先接觸產品和產品接觸面，這是無菌保證的基本原則。

            

**Mousehole (鼠洞口)：**RABS 上供容器或物料通過的小開口。AVS 需驗證這些開口處仍維持保護性氣流。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

AVS 就像用一面「空氣的鏡子」來看平時看不見的東西。正如我們在冬天呵氣可以「看見」氣流方向一樣，煙霧測試讓我們「看見」無塵室中原本不可見的空氣流動方向。但要注意一個矛盾：呵氣本身會改變周圍的氣流——同樣地，注入煙霧本身也會擾動我們想要觀察的環境。因此，如何「輕柔地呵氣」而不干擾原本的氣流，正是 AVS 的技術核心。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**煙霧產生的關鍵要求：**

            

                
- **不可使用甘油基霧化器**——會留下油性殘留物，影響設備性能與人員安全

                
- **推薦使用：**乾冰、WFI 蒸汽化、去離子水霧化、或液氮

                
- **注入角度：**約 45° 逆向氣流方向，速度要慢，避免因注入動作本身造成紊流

                
- **注入位置：**盡量靠近工作高度上方，但不要太靠近 HEPA 過濾器以避免堵塞

            

        

        

            

#### 攝影記錄的 GMP 要求

            

AVS 影片是正式的 GMP 記錄，必須符合數據完整性 (Data Integrity) 要求：

            

                
- 影片開頭應拍攝時鐘顯示日期時間

                
- 使用 2-4 個攝影角度，提供近似三維的氣流觀察

                
- 多角度影片應同步時間軸，便於並排比對

                
- 如後製剪輯，原始影片檔案必須保留（視為原始數據）

                
- 背景不應有不相關的活動（維修、清潔等）

            

        

        

            

#### 執行頻率的事件驅動原則

            

AVS 的重新執行頻率**不是基於時間**，而是基於**事件**——當設備或製程發生變更時才需重新執行。這與傳統「每年重做一次」的思維不同。但公司仍應定期評估是否需要重做，考量因素包括：

            

                
- 製程/設施變更的累積效應

                
- 影片拍攝品質是否可以提升

                
- 煙霧產生技術是否已改進

            

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**「彩排」的重要性：**文件特別建議在正式 AVS 前進行 dress rehearsal（彩排）。在 CDMO 環境中，這一步至關重要——因為 AVS 涉及多個部門協作（生產、QA、工程、微生物），任何溝通不良都可能導致影片需要重拍，浪費寶貴的潔淨室時間和資源。

            

**最大線速要求：**文件指出充填線以最大速度運行時需要進行 AVS，因為高速運轉的設備可能影響保護性氣流。CDMO 在進行產能擴充時，務必將此納入驗證規劃。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼煙霧的注入方向建議逆向（約 45°）於氣流方向？如果順向注入會發生什麼問題？

                
2. 文件建議在 RABS 內外分別注入煙霧。從 RABS 內部注入時，要觀察什麼？從外部注入時又要觀察什麼？

                
3. 為什麼 AVS 影片被視為 GMP 記錄？如果影片中出現操作人員未正確著裝的畫面，會有什麼影響？

            

        

    

## Q 2.4 Personnel Passage Through Grade A RABS

    

        

## 原文內容 Original Text

        

### Q 2.4. What are the considerations for facility layout design regarding acceptable personnel passage through the Grade A restricted access barrier system (RABS)?

        

**Recommendation**

        

Using a conveyor swing arm to lift the process line and doors that close into both sides to protect the line can allow the movement of operators from one side of the line to the other in cases where it is not possible to have two entrances into the room from the Grade B corridor. This movement should always be performed only after the impacted section of the line has been cleared of vials and is preferable in a section of the line where the units have already been filled and are fully stoppered. After personnel passage through the swing conveyor, a disinfection of the RABS interior/swing conveyor is required.

        

The environment immediately adjacent to the RABS may be designed to provide unidirectional airflow. This will provide protection to the glove ports and the interior of the doors when opened to performed inherent interventions (i.e., sterile equipment installation) or rare open-door corrective interventions. Computational Fluid Design (CFD) modeling may determine the need to have small rigid polycarbonate sheets extending from the ceiling to the top of the door height to ensure the airflow is unidirectional providing the desired protection.

        

**Rationale**

        

The movement of the swing arm might create turbulence in the surrounding air. Every effort must be made to prevent air external to the RABS from entering the RABS to protect units that are not yet integral from contamination.

        

Using smaller HEPA curtains that reach down to door height would provide some directionality and flush airflow without introducing risk to operators or materials.

    

    

        

## 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Conveyor Swing Arm (輸送帶擺臂)：**一種工程解決方案，允許將製程線路的一段抬起，讓操作人員從產線一側通行到另一側。這是在設施佈局無法提供兩個獨立入口時的替代方案。

            

**Computational Fluid Dynamics / CFD (計算流體力學)：**利用電腦模擬來分析空氣流動模式。在 RABS 設計中，CFD 可用於評估是否需要在天花板到門頂之間安裝聚碳酸酯導流板，以確保氣流維持單向性。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像 RABS 充填線就像一條河流上的橋——當人員需要從河的一側到另一側時，不能直接涉水而過（那會攪動河水、帶入污染）。Conveyor swing arm 就像一座可升降的吊橋，先把「河流」（產品輸送帶）抬起來，清空河道中的「船隻」（瓶子），然後讓人員快速通過。通過後，還需要「清理橋面」（消毒 RABS 內部）才能恢復通行。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**人員通行的三大前提條件：**

            

                
- **清線：**受影響區段的瓶子必須全部清除

                
- **優先選擇已密封區段：**最好在產品已充填且已加塞（fully stoppered）的區段通過

                
- **通行後消毒：**必須對 RABS 內部和擺臂進行消毒

            

            

**設施設計的根本原則：**理想的設施佈局應提供從 Grade B 走廊進入房間的兩個獨立入口，使操作人員無需穿越產線。只有在現有設施無法實現此佈局時，才應考慮 swing arm 方案。這再次體現了「設計優先」的 Quality by Design (QbD) 精神。

        

        

            

#### CFD 模擬的價值

            

CFD 建模不僅用於設計階段，還可以：

            

                
- 評估聚碳酸酯導流板的安裝位置和尺寸

                
- 模擬 swing arm 移動時產生的紊流範圍

                
- 驗證開門操作期間 UDAF 的保護效果

                
- 減少實體 mock-up 測試的次數，降低驗證成本

            

            

對 CDMO 而言，投資 CFD 建模可以在設施改造前預測潛在問題，避免昂貴的實體修改。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

在 CDMO 的設施規劃中，人員動線設計是初期就必須解決的問題。如果佈局設計導致操作人員經常需要穿越 Grade A 區域，每次通行都會產生額外的消毒時間和清線操作，直接影響產能利用率 (OEE)。因此，在新設施設計或舊設施改造的資本預算評估中，應將「雙走廊/雙入口」的投資與「swing arm + 每次通行損失的產能」進行總擁有成本 (TCO) 分析。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 為什麼人員通行優先選擇在「已充填且已加塞」的區段？如果在未加塞的區段通行，風險會如何改變？

                
2. 文件提到 CFD 模擬可以決定是否需要安裝聚碳酸酯導流板。請描述這些導流板的作用原理。

            

        

    

    

### 本節重點回顧 Section Summary

    

        
- **房間分級：**RABS 周圍環境的最低分級為 Grade B，這是 FDA/EMA 的強制要求。在 RABS 門區域可能需要更嚴格的管控，因為 RABS 不像隔離器那樣完全密封。

        
- **延伸 UDAF 監測：**RABS 門外的延伸 UDAF 區域需要動態監測策略——門關閉時按 Grade B 監測，門開啟時按「加嚴 Grade B」監測，限值應基於風險評估定義。

        
- **氣流可視化研究 (AVS)：**這是驗證 First Air 和 UDAF 保護的核心工具。關鍵要點包括：避免甘油基煙霧、逆向 45° 注入、多角度攝影、事件驅動的重新執行頻率，以及影片作為 GMP 記錄的數據完整性要求。

        
- **人員通道設計：**理想設計應避免人員穿越 Grade A 區域。必要時可使用 conveyor swing arm 方案，但必須遵守清線、選擇已密封區段、通行後消毒等前提條件。CFD 建模是優化設施氣流保護的重要工具。

    

↑

## Topic 3: Personnel 人員 (p41-p47)

# Topic 3: Personnel

    

主題三：人員管理

    

PDA Points to Consider No. 12 (2025): RABS | p41 - p47 | Q3.1 - Q3.4

    

### 本章學習目標

    

        
- 理解 RABS 操作人員手套消毒的重要性及其在污染控制策略 (CCS) 中的角色

        
- 掌握無菌操作人員四階段資格認證體系 (Level 1-4) 的完整流程

        
- 區分開門操作 (open-door intervention) 與關門操作 (closed-door intervention) 的人員資格要求差異

        
- 了解已認證介入操作 (qualified intervention) 與未認證介入操作 (unqualified intervention) 的管理策略

    

    

### 本章內容導覽

    

        Q3.1 手套消毒
        Q3.2 人員資格認證
        Q3.3 開門/關門操作資格區分
        Q3.4 已認證/未認證介入操作
    

Q 3.1 Operator Glove Disinfection | 操作手套消毒

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Q 3.1. Should operator gloves be disinfected prior to entering the restricted access barrier system (RABS) gloves?**

        

**Recommendation**

        

Disinfection of operator gloves prior to entry into the RABS gloves is an important component of the CCS and should be undertaken prior to each entry into the RABS gloves.

        

Gloved hands should be disinfected with an approved disinfectant (e.g., sterile isopropanol) prior to donning the RABS gloves (1, 4). The disinfectant can be applied by spraying. It is considered a basic and vital element of hygiene and cleanroom practices to minimize contamination risk or the transfer of contaminants within the clean room in general. It is also important that the risk of transfer of contamination from one operator to another is also considered and mitigated as part of the overall CCS.

        

Since RABS gloves are typically shared by more than one operator, the risk of contamination transfer from one operator to another through the shared use of the RABS gloves should be minimized by sanitizing the operator's own gloves before they enter into the glove ports or after exiting from the glove ports. The risk identified above (multiple operators using same gloves) is with reference to mitigating risk of contamination transfer between operators. Of course, the risk of product contamination requires equal consideration.

        

**Rationale**

        

RABS gloves are an integral design element and form part of the physical barrier that enables product protection by separating operators from the process.

        

Disinfection of gloves worn underneath RABS gloves will reduce the microbial load within the RABS gloves, in contrast to nondisinfected gloves. In the case of a pinhole in a RABS glove, a reduced microbial load on the inside of the RABS glove will reduce the chance of microbial ingress into the RABS Grade A environment (14).

        

RABS gloves are not infallible and, with continued use, may become worn, torn, or perforated and, hence, may potentially compromise the integrity of the system. While controls, including visual inspection (pre- and post-interventions of use) of gloves, provide for some degree of detection of holes or leaks, the identification of a leak through glove integrity-testing is usually undertaken post-batch or post-campaign manufacturing. This requires a retrospective assessment to determine the impact on the batch in the event of a confirmed glove-integrity breach.

        

For closed-door interventions that require the use of the RABS gloves, the risk profile associated with a potential breach of the Grade A RABS environment owing to a RABS glove integrity failure is high. This can be further compounded in the absence of operator glove disinfection, since the physical barrier between the operator hand (normally afforded through integral RABS gloves) and the Grade A environment is breached. A vector for microbiological contamination is thereby created, with risk profile reduced by ensuring adequate glove disinfection.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**RABS Glove Disinfection (RABS 手套消毒)：**這是 RABS 操作中最基本但也最容易被忽視的步驟。操作人員在將手伸入 RABS 手套之前，必須先用核准的消毒劑（如無菌異丙醇）對自己的無塵室手套進行消毒。

            

**為什麼「每次」都要做？**因為 RABS 手套通常是多人共用的。操作員 A 使用後，操作員 B 接著使用同一副 RABS 手套 —— 如果 A 的手套帶有微生物，這些微生物會留在 RABS 手套內表面，等 B 進入時就可能造成交叉污染。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

想像共用的 RABS 手套就像醫院裡共用的手術手套架。即使手術室（Grade A 區域）本身是無菌的，如果每位外科醫生在戴上手術手套前不先洗手消毒，那手套內部就會成為細菌的「中繼站」，從一位醫生傳給下一位。

            

更危險的是，如果手套上有一個肉眼看不見的針孔（pinhole），未消毒的手上的細菌就會直接滲入無菌區域 —— 就像防水手套破洞後，手就會被水浸濕一樣。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**深層防禦 (Defense in Depth) 思維：**手套完整性測試通常是在批次或批次活動結束後才進行的。這意味著如果手套在生產過程中破損，你只能在事後才發現。此時，事前的手套消毒就成為了關鍵的「最後一道防線」。

            

                
- 手套消毒 = 降低手套內部微生物負載

                
- 手套完整性測試 = 事後確認手套是否有破損

                
- 兩者結合 = 即使手套破損，因為內部微生物量低，對產品的風險也被最小化

            

            

這正是 Contamination Control Strategy (CCS) 的精髓：不依賴單一控制措施，而是建立多層保護。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 的挑戰：**在 CDMO 環境中，不同客戶的產品可能使用同一條 RABS 充填線，操作人員在換班或產品切換時更需要嚴格執行手套消毒。建議在 SOP 中明確規定：

            

                
- 每次進入 RABS 手套前必須噴灑無菌 IPA

                
- 操作員交接時，接手者必須在進入前消毒

                
- 在 CCS 文件中記錄手套消毒的頻率與方法

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 如果一位操作員在未消毒手套的情況下進行了 RABS 關門操作，事後發現該 RABS 手套有針孔破損，你會如何評估對批次的影響？

                
2. 為什麼文件強調消毒劑可以用「噴灑」方式施用？與浸泡相比有什麼實務優勢？

            

        

    

Q 3.2 Personnel Qualification | 人員資格認證

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Q 3.2. How are personnel qualified for executing interventions?**

        

**Recommendation**

        

For qualification of personnel for open-door and/or closed-door interventions, an intervention management program should be established. Typically, a phase-wise approach is followed to increase operator proficiency.

        

**Level 1 – Training**

        

A well-rounded personnel qualification training program should include, but not be limited to, the following:

        

            
- Basic elements of microbiology and hygiene with specific focus on cleanroom practices (slow, deliberate movements of body and arms/gloves), principles about contamination control, First Air concept, good aseptic working techniques (i.e., in particular during RABS open-door interventions), protection of sterile products and critical surfaces, and the potential safety implications to the patient if a product is not sterile.

            
- Visual airflow studies should be used in training to support the understanding of operator interventions in the aseptic space. Virtual reality-based training modules may be used as a best practice in training to assess operators' skills and mitigate risks by providing immersive, interactive simulations that help them practice real-life situations in a controlled environment.

            
- Aseptic gowning and cleanroom behavior training is to be provided. The trainee should perform dry runs of gowning and degowning under the supervision of an experienced trainer, showing that the trainee is able to perform the gowning process appropriately and consistently. Those dry runs can be performed in suitable office spaces or otherwise easy-to-access rooms. Gowning qualification can be initiated in conjunction with a trainer after successful completion of the basic elements of microbiology and cleanroom behavior aspects outlined above.

        

        

**Level 2 – Gowning Qualification Followed by Demonstration**

        

The aseptic-gowning procedure should be confirmed by a visual and microbial (plating with contact plates) assessment, and the trainee's capability to don the complete sterile gown in an aseptic manner to allow entry in the aseptic area should be evaluated.

        

**Demonstration of Assembly/Machine Setup, Interventions, and Filling Operation**

        

Training is required on site-specific standard procedures, on machine parts setup and interventions, with the help of applicable dynamic airflow visualization studies. Training can be staggered based on intervention complexity, wherein operators first demonstrate competency to perform less complex interventions prior to moving to more complex interventions. Alternatively, the training may be certified as one block, where proficiency in all relevant interventions (irrespective of complexity) must be demonstrated for the operator to be certified.

        

Personnel should observe the production activities (setup and interventions) during routine commercial batch-manufacturing from the view windows or by viewing remote cameras without entering into the aseptic area. This can be done in parallel with Level 2 training, with supervisory monitoring by experienced and qualified personnel.

        

Personnel should simulate machine setup and interventions in the aseptic core, with the supervision of qualified personnel, by performing interventions in Grade A when there is no commercial batch-manufacturing (e.g., after completion of the routine commercial batch operations, prior to cleaning of the filling line). Assessment of nonviable and viable particle-monitoring during those simulations may be considered. The number of dry runs to be considered should be based on personnel skill set and prior experience before allowing participation in an APS run.

        

**Level 3 – Practical Assessment in Smaller-Batch and Regular APS**

        

After completing Levels 1 and 2, the personnel should perform setup and interventions with participation in an APS (1, 4, 7, 15). The run can be independent of routine APS, or it can be a routine APS run. The APS run may be smaller or of routine size depending on the size of the operation, the number of personnel to be qualified, and the process complexity oRABS/cRABS and open- or closed-interventions.

        

A bracketing approach can be applied for setup operations in the case of similarities in manipulations and interventions during the media manipulation run for qualifying more than one operator within the same run, based on the risk-based approach. However, attention should be paid to the number of units filled by an individual operator to be representative of the actual commercial operation.

        

Choosing a setup process that is more challenging to perform or more complex in execution and grouping interventions to perform with different sets of tools (e.g., using short or long forceps, stopper/seal track adjustments, needle adjustment) is recommended.

        

For open-door versus closed-door interventions, all open-door interventions and closed-door interventions that are classified as high risk within site-risk assessment documents should be chosen to be performed. When certifying the personnel to perform the aseptic processing activities in commercial batches, the same procedures that were qualified in the APS run should be chosen. Upon the successful result of APS, the data compliance monitoring (continuous viable and total particle), assessment of aseptic techniques, and the behavior of the operator(s) to be qualified for performing aseptic operations, the operator should be qualified.

        

Within lifecycle management, when any new open-door interventions are added to the system at later stages, quality management tools should ensure that the personnel are qualified to perform the additional interventions and the interventions have been simulated in APS runs, unless it has been otherwise documented in risk assessments with scientific rationale that the new intervention is like the qualified one.

        

**Level 4 – Ongoing Training and Assessment**

        

Upon successful completion of personnel qualification, the operator should be certified to perform aseptic operations, and their aseptic behavior should be monitored on a periodic/continuous basis until a sufficient level of experience is achieved. The assessment should evaluate if supervision of the newly qualified person can be reduced or if further training and additional assessment is required. It is recommended to qualify personnel annually, for both gowning and participation in APS runs.

        

**Disqualification of Aseptic Processing Personnel**

        

In the event when operators are considered disqualified, access to the aseptic area should be removed/prohibited until demonstration of successful requalification. The disqualification criteria may include:

        

            
1. Failure to qualify or meet periodic qualification requirements

            
2. Participation in an unsuccessful or failed APS, where their performance was identified as a cause or contribution to the failure

            
3. Repeated aseptic processing technique in a manner deemed unacceptable in relation to cleanroom or aseptic-process operations or functions

            
4. Failure to maintain gowning qualification

            
5. Failure to maintain training requirements

            
6. Repeated personnel monitoring excursions

            
7. Extended periods of inactivity or absence from the aseptic processing area

            
8. Other aspects of performance as identified by a supervisor (e.g., behavioral)

        

        

The requalification should be defined on the reason and relative risk associated with the disqualification.

        

**Rationale**

        

The performance of personnel-related activities, manipulations, and interventions in the RABS during aseptic operations can pose a risk to the sterility of the product or adversely affect it if it is not performed in an aseptic manner. Therefore, proper training and qualification of personnel with APS experience is a must.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Intervention Management Program (介入操作管理計畫)：**這不只是一份訓練清單，而是一套完整的人員能力發展體系。PDA 建議採用四階段漸進式方法，從基礎知識到實際操作，逐步建立操作人員的無菌操作能力。

            

**四階段認證體系：**

            

                
- **Level 1 - 訓練 (Training)：**微生物學基礎、無塵室行為規範、First Air 概念、穿衣練習

                
- **Level 2 - 穿衣認證 + 操作示範 (Gowning Qualification + Demonstration)：**通過微生物接觸板評估的穿衣認證，加上在非生產時段的模擬操作

                
- **Level 3 - APS 實務評估 (Practical Assessment in APS)：**參與無菌製程模擬 (APS)，在模擬條件下執行完整操作

                
- **Level 4 - 持續訓練與評估 (Ongoing Training)：**年度再認證，包含穿衣和 APS 參與

            

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這個四階段認證體系就像飛行員的培訓過程：

            

                
- **Level 1 (地面學校)：**學習航空理論、氣象學、飛行規則 —— 對應微生物學和無塵室基礎知識

                
- **Level 2 (模擬器訓練)：**在飛行模擬器中練習各種情境 —— 對應穿衣認證和在非生產時段的操作演練

                
- **Level 3 (教練隨行飛行)：**在真正的飛機上飛行，但有教練在旁 —— 對應在 APS 中的實際操作

                
- **Level 4 (定期複訓)：**即使是經驗豐富的機長也要定期通過飛行檢定 —— 對應年度再認證

            

            

就像飛行員不能跳過模擬器直接上飛機一樣，無菌操作人員也不能跳過任何階段。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**VR 訓練的前瞻性建議：**PDA 在此首次明確提到 Virtual Reality (VR) 訓練模組可作為最佳實踐。這是一個重要的產業趨勢信號 —— 未來法規檢查可能會將 VR 訓練視為先進的訓練工具。

            

**觀察學習的重要性：**Level 2 中特別提到人員應透過觀察窗或遠端攝影機觀察實際生產操作，而非直接進入無菌區域。這個「看但不碰」的階段非常重要，讓操作員在安全的環境中理解真實操作的節奏和複雜性。

        

        

            

#### 取消資格條件 Disqualification Criteria

            

文件列出了八項可能導致操作人員被取消資格的情況，這些條件涵蓋了三個維度：

            

                
- **技能衰退：**未通過定期認證、穿衣認證失效、長時間未進入無菌區

                
- **操作失誤：**APS 失敗且其表現被認定為原因、重複不當操作技術

                
- **監控異常：**重複出現人員監控偏差

            

            

特別注意第 7 項：「長時間不活動或缺席」。這意味著即使操作員之前完全合格，長時間未執行操作後也必須重新認證。許多 CDMO 在這一點上容易疏忽。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 的 Bracketing 策略：**文件提到可以對具有相似性的操作採用 Bracketing Approach（括弧法），在同一次 APS 中認證多位操作員。這對 CDMO 特別有價值：

            

                
- 選擇最具挑戰性的設備設定流程進行模擬

                
- 組合不同工具的操作（長鑷子、短鑷子、膠塞軌道調整等）

                
- 確保每位操作員充填的單位數量具有代表性

            

            

這樣可以減少 APS 執行次數，同時確保認證的嚴謹性 —— 對 CDMO 而言是成本效益的最佳平衡。

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 一位操作員因「長時間缺席」（6 個月未進入無菌區）被取消資格。重新認證時，你認為應該從 Level 幾開始？為什麼？

                
2. Level 2 訓練中提到可以在「辦公室空間」練習穿脫衣。這樣的練習環境是否足夠？與在實際無塵室中練習相比，各有什麼優缺點？

                
3. 文件建議年度再認證包含穿衣和 APS 參與。如果你的工廠一年只執行兩次常規 APS，但有 20 位操作員需要再認證，你會如何安排？

            

        

    

Q 3.3 Open-Door vs Closed-Door Qualification | 開門與關門操作資格區分

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Q 3.3. Is there a clear distinction between the operator qualification for closed- and open-door operator interventions, and are operators qualified for closed-door interventions allowed to perform open-door interventions (For operators qualified for specific tasks, e.g., primary operator, secondary operator, based on criticality)?**

        

**Recommendation**

        

After setup, open-door interventions should be rare events. The personnel authorized to conduct open-door line setup and permitted open-door interventions should be trained and qualified specifically for open-door interventions after they have been permitted to undertake closed-door interventions.

        

Requirements for qualification of open- and closed-door interventions should be clearly distinguished.

        

An operator qualified for closed-door intervention is **not allowed** to perform open-door intervention due to the risk factors associated with aseptic techniques and intervention type. But a person qualified for open-door interventions **can** be allowed to perform closed-door interventions due to the low risk and considering the similarities in the intervention process. However, this should be clearly documented in the site's quality risk assessment and CCS documents (1).

        

A qualified-operator list should clearly specify the personnel authorized to perform interventions into the Grade A environment, with open-, closed-, or both interventions and, within that category grouping, can be done based on the similarities (e.g., loading of stoppers and/or seals if the latter is performed in the RABS).

        

**Rationale**

        

Interventions should be designed and performed using proper aseptic techniques to minimize the risk of product contamination. Operators should be first performing closed-door interventions and gaining a skillset at a later stage to perform open-door interventions. (See Question 3.2 for additional information.)

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**資格不對稱性原則：**Q3.3 建立了一個非常重要的規則 —— 操作資格的「單向相容性」：

            
                
                    
                    
                    
                
| 操作員資格 | 可執行關門操作？ | 可執行開門操作？ |
| --- | --- | --- |
                
                    
                    
                    
                
| 僅認證關門操作 | 可以 | 不可以 |
                
                    
                    
                    
                
| 認證開門操作 | 可以 | 可以 |
            

            

邏輯很清楚：開門操作的風險遠高於關門操作，因為開門時 Grade A 環境直接暴露在 Grade B 背景中。能執行高風險操作的人，自然也能執行低風險操作，但反過來則不行。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

這就像駕駛執照的等級制度：持有大客車駕照的人可以開小客車，但只有小客車駕照的人不能開大客車。

            

開門操作就像開大客車 —— 需要更高的技能、更嚴格的訓練、更多的經驗。關門操作是小客車 —— 仍然需要基本資格，但風險等級較低。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**Qualified-Operator List (合格操作員清單) 的重要性：**

            

文件要求建立一份明確的「合格操作員清單」，這份清單必須：

            

                
- 清楚標示每位操作員被授權執行的操作類型（開門/關門/兩者）

                
- 在同一類別內，可根據操作的相似性進行分組（如：膠塞和密封件的裝載如果操作相似，可歸為一組）

                
- 必須記錄在品質風險評估和 CCS 文件中

            

            

在法規檢查時，檢查官經常會要求查看這份清單，並交叉比對當天在 RABS 內執行開門操作的人員是否確實在授權名單上。

        

        

            

#### 實務應用 Practical Application

            

**CDMO 的排班策略：**在 CDMO 的多產品環境中，確保每個班次至少有一位經認證的開門操作人員在場是非常重要的。建議：

            

                
- 建立分級操作員制度：Primary Operator（主操作員，具開門資格）和 Secondary Operator（副操作員，僅關門資格）

                
- 排班系統中加入資格檢查邏輯，確保開門操作人員的覆蓋率

                
- 設備設定（setup）階段需要開門操作，此時必須安排合格人員

            

        

        

            

#### 練習思考 Practice Questions

            

                
1. 在夜班期間，唯一具備開門操作資格的人員因突發狀況離開。此時發生了需要開門介入才能解決的設備故障。你會如何處理？

                
2. 文件提到開門操作資格的操作員「可以」執行關門操作，但需要記錄在 CCS 文件中。為什麼這個「向下相容」還需要正式文件記錄？

            

        

    

Q 3.4 Qualified vs Unqualified Interventions | 已認證與未認證介入操作

    

        

### 原文內容 Original Text

        

**Q 3.4. What are the recommendations for qualified and unqualified interventions?**

        

**Recommendation**

        

**Best Practices for Qualified Interventions**

        

Interventions should be conducted by trained and qualified personnel. (See Question 3.2 on how to qualify.)

        

An approved standard operating procedure (SOP) containing all defined interventions with step-by-step instructions, mitigation actions (if any), and images (where applicable) should exist (1, 4, 7, 15, 16). A dynamic AVS should be performed simulating all the listed interventions, and these studies should be repeated with a defined frequency as described in Question 2.3.

        

Simulation of all qualified interventions in routine APS should be performed on a rotational basis; its maximum frequency of occurrence in routine batch-manufacturing should be covered in an initial qualification run and semiannual qualification runs. A rotation policy can be defined in an internal-site risk management process but should occur at least annually.

        

**Management of Unqualified Interventions**

        

When an unqualified intervention occurs, a real-time risk-based impact assessment shall be performed (See Question 1.7 on how to risk assess). If the assessment determines the unqualified intervention can be performed, only authorized personnel (See Question 3.2 on authorized personnel) may execute the unqualified intervention. If the risk assessment does not support the intervention as safe, then the intervention should not proceed and the appropriate steps to end the batch should be taken. As part of batch release, the impact of the unqualified intervention must be assessed for quality and compliance on the batch.

        

Unqualified interventions identified to become qualified interventions shall have AVS to demonstrate unidirectional airflow and preservation of First Air are not impacted. The unqualified intervention will then be included in the ongoing APS program and upon successful completion the intervention can be added to the local procedure. Unqualified interventions that are similar to qualified interventions may not require additional AVS execution or inclusion in the APS program, to become a qualified intervention, if proven equivalent with supporting technical and scientific rationale. In certain situations, unqualified interventions may not be recommended to become a qualified intervention, based upon special events, and will not require simulation in AVS and APS programs.

        

**Rationale**

        

Interventions should be designed and performed using proper aseptic techniques to minimize impact to the production environment and the risk of product contamination. An unqualified intervention does not have sufficient data to demonstrate the capability of control, hence, simulating the unqualified intervention in APS testing to demonstrate the process capability is recommended.

    

    

        

### 導師解析 Tutorial Commentary

        

            

#### 核心概念解析 Key Concepts

            

**Qualified Intervention (已認證介入操作)：**指已經過完整驗證流程的操作 —— 有 SOP 文件、已做過 AVS（氣流可視化研究）證明不影響 First Air、已在 APS（無菌製程模擬）中模擬並成功完成。這些操作是「預期中會發生的」，系統已證明可以安全執行。

            

**Unqualified Intervention (未認證介入操作)：**指尚未經過上述完整驗證流程的操作。這是「意料之外的」操作，例如設備出現從未遇過的故障，需要一種新的處理方式。

            

**關鍵區別：**「未認證」不等於「禁止」。文件建立了一套完整的決策流程來處理未認證操作。

        

        

            

#### 比喻說明 Analogy

            

把這想像成一家航空公司的飛行手冊：

            

                
- **Qualified Interventions（標準操作程序）：**就像飛行手冊中已列出的所有標準和緊急程序 —— 引擎失效怎麼辦、液壓系統故障怎麼辦。這些都已經過模擬器訓練和反覆演練。

                
- **Unqualified Interventions（未知情況）：**就像遇到飛行手冊中沒有記載的全新狀況。機長必須即時評估風險（real-time risk assessment），決定是否能安全處理，還是應該返航（停止批次）。

            

            

而且，如果某個「未知情況」開始頻繁出現，航空公司就應該把它寫入手冊（將 unqualified 升級為 qualified），進行模擬器訓練（AVS + APS），讓所有飛行員都學會處理。

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Key Notes

            

**未認證介入操作的決策樹：**

            

                
1. **即時風險評估：**發生未認證操作時，立即執行風險評估

                
2. **決策分叉：**
                    

                        
    - 風險可接受 → 由授權人員執行，但必須在批次放行時評估其影響

                        
    - 風險不可接受 → 不執行操作，採取適當步驟結束批次

                    

                

                
3. **後續處理：**決定該未認證操作是否應升級為已認證操作
                    

                        
    - 需升級 → 執行 AVS 驗證 + 納入 APS 計畫

                        
    - 與現有已認證操作相似 → 可透過技術合理性證明等效，不一定需要額外 AVS/APS

                        
    - 屬於特殊事件 → 不建議升級為已認證操作

                    

                

            

        

        

            

#### 重點提示 Rotation Policy

            

**已認證操作的輪替模擬策略：**文件要求所有已認證操作都必須在常規 APS 中進行模擬，但採用「輪替」方式：

            

                
- 初始認證 APS：涵蓋操作在常規生產中的最大發生頻率

                
- 半年度認證 APS：輪替模擬不同的操作

                
- 輪替週期：每個操作至少每年被模擬一次
